121.2(1): pa tshe yi bar do la rang rig lhag mthong du shar ba dang / 'jig pa dus kyi bar do 
121.3(1): la bon nyid 'od gsal du sangs rgyas pa'i 'bras bu thob par 'gyur ro/ /de ltar na/

121.6(1): la rtogs shig /steng lha yi srid pa la skye ba'i sems can rnams kyang / bskal pa 
121.7(1): bzang po'i sangs rgyas stong rtsa gnyis kyi mtshan brjod pa 'di la mi nyan mi rtogs na/

121.13(1): mongs pa rang rig lhag mthong du shar ba dang / 'jig pa dus kyi bar do la bon

121.17(1): la yongs su rtogs shig /bar mi'i srid pa la bskyed pa'i sems can rnams kyis 
121.18(1): bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas stong rtsa gnyis kyi mtshan brjod pa 'di la mi nyan mi

121.20(1): rten gyi khams su byon pa dang mi 'phrad par 'gyur ro/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bar mi'i 
121.21(1): srid pa la bskyed pa'i sems can rnams kyang 'di la mnyan par bya'o/ /'di la

123.21(1): sa ston dpal 'byor gto rgyal dang / gshen rab thang ma me sgron dang / gtsug

182.3(1): yab ni dbyings sgrol 'od de bskyed pa'i yum/ 'phrul dga' ma zhes bya ste sprul pa'i 
182.4(1): sras/ tshangs rgyal tog ces bya ba rim gro pa/ bram ze ha rgyal yin te ye shes lha/
182.5(1): 'od lha ye spungs zhes bya srid pa'i mchog /thang bskyed 'od ces bya ba 'dus pa'i 
182.6(1): 'khor/ g.yung drung sems dpa' sum brgya drug cu'o/ /tshe lo'i tshad kyang sum stong 
182.7(1): bzhi brgya'o/ /g.yung drung bon ni lo grangs gcig khri'i bar/ de tshe gnas 'gyur sku 
182.8(1): gdung mchod rten yang / rin chen gdugs dang lhab lhub mdzes pa yi/ 'jig 
182.9(1): rten dpag tshad rnam grangs ril gcig zad/ 'gro don tshad kyang dgu stong dgu 
182.10(1): brgya'o/ /sangs rgyas de yi bstan pa yongs rdzogs la/ bskal pa gcig gi sems 
182.11(1): can 'dren par 'gyur/ de bzhin sangs rgyas gtsug rgyal dbyings rgyan gyi/ skye ba'i 
182.12(1): yul dang grong khyer zhing khams ni/ 'ol mo gling chen sham po lha rtse'i mkhar/ yab ni 
182.13(1): dbyings drag rgyal yin bskyed pa'i yum/ gzhi brtan ma zhes bya ste sprul pa'i sras/
182.14(1): ting nam dpag zhes bya ste rim gro pa/ bram ze mu ling yin te ye shes lha/ 'od lha 
182.15(1): don gsal zhes bya srid pa'i mchog /g.yung drung sems dpa' bye ba dgu stong ngo / /
182.16(1): sku tshe'i tshad kyang bye ba 'bum phrag khri/ g.yung drung bon yang bye ba phrag bcu'i bar/
182.17(1): de tshe gnas 'gyur sku gdung mchod rten yang / rin chen sna lnga gdugs chen rgyang 
182.18(1): grags 'bum/ 'jig rten dpag tshad yongs su khyab 'gyur la/ 'gro don tshad kyang 
182.19(1): bye ba dung phyur te/ sangs rgyas de yi bstan pa yongs rdzogs la/ bskal pa gcig gi 
182.20(1): sems can 'dren par 'gyur/ de bzhin du/ sangs rgyas 'bum gshen gyer rmang gi/
182.21(1): skye ba'i yul dang grong khyer zhing khams ni/ 'ol mo gling chen sham po lha rtse'i mkhar/
183.1(1): yab ni gyer ling thang yin bskyed pa'i yum/ 'od 'byams ma zhes bya ba sprul pa'i 
183.2(1): sras/ mu rum rtogs ces bya ba rim gro pa/ bram ze lha mkhan yin te ye shes lha/
183.3(1): 'od lha gong khri zhes bya srid pa'i mchog /dpal nam shugs ldan yin te 'dus pa'i 
183.4(1): 'khor/ g.yung drung sems dpa' bye ba sum stong ngo / /sku tshe'i tshad kyang lo grangs 
183.5(1): 'bum phrag yin/ g.yung drung bon ni bye ba phrag lnga'i bar/ de tshe gnas 'gyur sku 
183.6(1): gdung mchod rten yang / rin chen gdugs dang me tog rgyang grags khri/ 'jig rten 
183.7(1): dpag tshad rnam grangs rgyas 'gyur la/ 'gro don tshad kyang 'bum phrag brgyad stong 
183.8(1): ste/ sangs rgyas de yi bstan pa yongs rdzogs la/ bskal pa gcig gi sems can 
183.9(1): 'dren par 'gyur/ de bzhin sangs rgyas don gyi sems gsal gyi/ skye ba'i yul dang 
183.10(1): grong khyer zhing khams ni/ 'ol mo gling chen sham po lha rtse'i mkhar/ yab ni don rgyal 
183.11(1): yin te bskyed pa'i yum/ mkha' la bde zhes bya ste sprul pa'i sras/ grub pa rtags 
183.12(1): ces bya ste rim gro pa/ bram ze dge sbyangs yin te ye shes lha/ 'od lha 'bar drag ces 
183.13(1): bya srid pa'i mchog /'phrul sangs rtogs pa yin te 'dus pa'i 'khor/ g.yung drung

381.18(1): du ma rnyed kyang bris pa'i chad lhag sogs kyis gcig mtshungs med pa dang / nged zhus 
381.19(1): sgrig pa tsho'i mkhyen dpyod tshad brgal can min pa bcas dang rjes 'gro byas pas nor 
381.20(1): 'khrul gyis bslad pa'ang yod nges pas/ rjes gzigs mkhan rnam pas su dang gang la 
381.21(1): khag dkri med pa rang bstan rang skyong gi 'gan 'khri gtsang ma phrag tu khur ste bstan pa 
381.22(1): rin po che'i ched du nor 'khrul yo bsrang dag ther gnang ba'i skul ma zhu rgyu dang /
382.1(1): mthar don du nged [<<]g.yung drung bon gyi bka' brten dpe rnying phyogs bsgrigs khang [>>]
382.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
382.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
382.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
382.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
382.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
382.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
382.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
382.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan [(3)]bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
382.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
382.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
382.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
382.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
382.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
382.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
382.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
382.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
382.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
382.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi
